In the top right corner, there will be gray text that says "Show API key" click it.
It will display something like this: API key: 378ndug4j6hjbdgb5678dmg
Copy the random string, this is your API key.
Open termux
Do these commands

$cd shodan
$touch shodan-api.txt. <--- "touch" is a command that creates a file in your current directory, it doesn't mean touch the screen with your finger.
$echo "Shodan API key: <BzG6pXvl4EOW8R6ikmqIZRzdpKu4oAit>" > shodan-api.txt. <----- do not include < or > when you paste the API key, those are just to show that user supplied input is needed.
Your shodan API key is now safe in this txt file for future use.
$ shodan init <BzG6pXvl4EOW8R6ikmqIZRzdpKu4oAit>
